title: ProFields
description: Standalone field primitives for forms — Input, Password, Textarea, Digit, Select, DatePicker, Upload, Captcha, ArrayField, ObjectField, and more.
---

## Installation

<CodeTabs>

<TabsList>
  <TabsTrigger value="cli">Command</TabsTrigger>
  <TabsTrigger value="manual">Manual</TabsTrigger>
</TabsList>

<TabsContent value="cli">

```bash
npx @draco-china/shadcn-pro add pro-fields
```

</TabsContent>

<TabsContent value="manual">

<Steps className="mb-0 pt-2">

<Step>Install the following dependencies:</Step>

```bash
bun add date-fns lucide-react
```

<Step>
  Copy and paste the component files into your project under
  `components/pro/pro-fields/`.
</Step>

<Step>Update the import paths to match your project setup.</Step>

</Steps>

</TabsContent>

</CodeTabs>

## Usage

Every field is a plain React/shadcn component. Simple fields preserve the underlying shadcn/ui prop surface where practical; shadcn-pro adds only small behaviors such as `allowClear`, prefix/suffix slots, options mapping, and composed field layouts. Formily adapters live under `pro-form/formily-fields`, so schema-driven forms can use the same field primitives without making the base fields depend on Formily.

```tsx
import { Input } from "@/components/pro/pro-fields/input"

export default function Example() {
  return <Input placeholder="Enter username" allowClear />
}
```

For schema-driven forms, install `pro-form` and import the Formily adapters from `pro-form/formily-fields`.

```tsx
import { createForm } from "@formily/core"
import { Field, FormProvider } from "@formily/react"

import { FormItem } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/form-item"
import { FormilyInput } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/formily-fields"

const form = createForm()

export default function Example() {
  return (
    <FormProvider form={form}>
      <Field
        name="username"
        title="Username"
        decorator={[FormItem]}
        component={[FormilyInput, { placeholder: "Enter username" }]}
      />
    </FormProvider>
  )
}
```

---

## FacetedFilter

A Popover + Checkbox filter component designed for faceted search — auto-used by `ProTable` when `meta.filters` is set on a column, and available standalone for forms or custom toolbars. Supports single-select and multi-select modes.

### API Reference

| Prop          | Type                                | Default     | Description                                              |
| ------------- | ----------------------------------- | ----------- | -------------------------------------------------------- |
| `value`       | `string \| string[]`                | —           | Controlled selected value(s)                             |
| `onChange`    | `(value: string \| string[] \| undefined) => void` | — | Change handler                              |
| `options`     | `{ label: string; value: string; icon?: ComponentType }[]` | `[]` | Filter options                      |
| `placeholder` | `string`                            | `'Filter...'` | Button label / search placeholder                      |
| `mode`        | `'single' \| 'multi'`               | `'multi'`   | Single-select (radio-like) or multi-select (checkbox)    |
| `className`   | `string`                            | —           | Additional CSS classes                                   |

```tsx
import { FacetedFilter } from "@/components/pro/pro-fields/faceted-filter"

<FacetedFilter
  placeholder="Status"
  mode="multi"
  options={[
    { label: "Active", value: "active" },
    { label: "Inactive", value: "inactive" },
  ]}
  value={selected}
  onChange={setSelected}
/>
```

  name="pro-fields-slider-demo"

### API Reference

| Prop        | Type                      | Default | Description              |
| ----------- | ------------------------- | ------- | ------------------------ |
| `value`     | `number`                  | —       | Controlled value         |
| `onChange`  | `(value: number) => void` | —       | Change handler           |
| `min`       | `number`                  | `0`     | Minimum value            |
| `max`       | `number`                  | `100`   | Maximum value            |
| `step`      | `number`                  | `1`     | Step increment           |
| `showValue` | `boolean`                 | `false` | Show current value badge |
| `disabled`  | `boolean`                 | `false` | Disable interaction      |
| `className` | `string`                  | —       | Additional CSS classes   |

## Cascader

<ComponentPreview
  name="pro-fields-cascader-demo"
  previewClassName="min-h-[300px] items-start p-6"
  align="start"
/>

### API Reference

| Prop          | Type                        | Default       | Description            |
| ------------- | --------------------------- | ------------- | ---------------------- |
| `value`       | `string[]`                  | —             | Selected path values   |
| `onChange`    | `(value: string[]) => void` | —             | Change handler         |
| `options`     | `CascaderOption[]`          | `[]`          | Nested option tree     |
| `placeholder` | `string`                    | `'Select...'` | Placeholder text       |
| `disabled`    | `boolean`                   | `false`       | Disable interaction    |
| `className`   | `string`                    | —             | Additional CSS classes |

```ts
interface CascaderOption {
  label: string
  value: string
  disabled?: boolean
  children?: CascaderOption[]
}
```

## TreeSelect

<ComponentPreview
  name="pro-fields-tree-select-demo"
  previewClassName="min-h-[320px] items-start p-6"
  align="start"
/>

### API Reference

| Prop          | Type                        | Default       | Description                                                         |
| ------------- | --------------------------- | ------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `value`       | `string[]`                  | —             | Selected node values                                                |
| `onChange`    | `(value: string[]) => void` | —             | Change handler                                                      |
| `options`     | `TreeSelectOption[]`        | `[]`          | Nested tree data                                                    |
| `placeholder` | `string`                    | `'Select...'` | Placeholder text                                                    |
| `multiple`    | `boolean`                   | `false`       | Allow multiple selection                                            |
| `allowClear`  | `boolean`                   | `false`       | Show a clear button when the field has a value and is not required. |
| `disabled`    | `boolean`                   | `false`       | Disable interaction                                                 |
| `className`   | `string`                    | —             | Additional CSS classes                                              |

```ts
interface TreeSelectOption {
  label: string
  value: string
  disabled?: boolean
  children?: TreeSelectOption[]
}
```

## Upload

<ComponentPreview
  name="pro-fields-upload-demo"
  previewClassName="min-h-[320px] items-start p-6"
  align="start"
/>

### API Reference

| Prop          | Type                            | Default                     | Description          |
| ------------- | ------------------------------- | --------------------------- | -------------------- |
| `value`       | `UploadFile[]`                  | —                           | Controlled file list |
| `onChange`    | `(files: UploadFile[]) => void` | —                           | Change handler       |
| `accept`      | `string`                        | —                           | Accepted MIME types  |
| `multiple`    | `boolean`                       | `false`                     | Allow multiple files |
| `maxCount`    | `number`                        | —                           | Maximum file count   |
| `disabled`    | `boolean`                       | `false`                     | Disable interaction  |
| `placeholder` | `string`                        | `'Click or drag to upload'` | Drop zone label      |

```ts
interface UploadFile {
  uid: string
  name: string
  url?: string
  status?: "uploading" | "done" | "error"
  size?: number
}
```

## Captcha

<ComponentPreview
  name="pro-fields-captcha-demo"
  previewClassName="min-h-[260px] items-start p-6"
  align="start"
/>

### API Reference

| Prop              | Type          | Default           | Description                                                                                    |
| ----------------- | ------------- | ----------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `value`           | `string`      | —                 | Controlled input value                                                                         |
| `onChange`        | `(e) => void` | —                 | Input change handler                                                                           |
| `onRefresh`       | `() => void`  | —                 | Called when refresh button clicked                                                             |
| `captchaUrl`      | `string`      | —                 | Image URL for image captcha; when provided, the visual captcha is shown after the input.       |
| `captchaText`     | `string`      | —                 | Text to display as visual captcha; when provided, the visual captcha is shown after the input. |
| `buttonText`      | `string`      | `'Get code'`      | Text for the trailing send-code button when no visual captcha is provided.                     |
| `countdown`       | `number`      | `60`              | Countdown seconds after clicking the trailing send-code button. Set `0` to disable countdown.  |
| `placeholder`     | `string`      | `'Enter captcha'` | Input placeholder                                                                              |
| `disabled`        | `boolean`     | `false`           | Disable interaction                                                                            |
| `inputClassName`  | `string`      | —                 | Additional className for the input.                                                            |
| `buttonClassName` | `string`      | —                 | Additional className for the trailing send-code button.                                        |
| `className`       | `string`      | —                 | Additional CSS classes                                                                         |

## Core Fields

The following fields cover the full ProFields surface. Use the standalone field primitives directly, or use the matching Formily adapter from `pro-form/formily-fields` when building schema-driven forms.

### Input

<ComponentPreview
  name="pro-fields-input-demo"
  previewClassName="min-h-[160px] items-start p-6"
  align="start"
/>

```tsx
<Field
  name="email"
  title="Email"
  decorator={[FormItem]}
  component={[
    FormilyInput,
    { placeholder: "you@example.com", type: "email", allowClear: true },
  ]}
/>
```

### Textarea

<ComponentPreview
  name="pro-fields-textarea-demo"
  previewClassName="min-h-[200px] items-start p-6"
  align="start"
/>

```tsx
<Field
  name="bio"
  title="Bio"
  decorator={[FormItem]}
  component={[
    FormilyTextarea,
    { rows: 4, placeholder: "Tell us about yourself" },
  ]}
/>
```

### Password

<ComponentPreview
  name="pro-fields-password-demo"
  previewClassName="min-h-[160px] items-start p-6"
  align="start"
/>

```tsx
<Field
  name="password"
  title="Password"
  decorator={[FormItem]}
  component={[FormilyPassword, { placeholder: "Enter password" }]}
/>
```

### Digit

### ArrayField

Drag-to-reorder list with built-in state management. Supports controlled (`value` + `onChange`) and uncontrolled (`defaultValue`) usage.

<ComponentPreview
  name="pro-fields-array-field-demo"
  previewClassName="min-h-[280px] items-start p-6"
  align="start"
/>

| Prop | Type | Default | Description |
|------|------|---------|-------------|
| `value` | `TItem[]` | — | Controlled array value |
| `onChange` | `(value: TItem[]) => void` | — | Called on any change |
| `defaultValue` | `TItem[]` | `[]` | Initial value (uncontrolled) |
| `newItem` | `() => TItem` | `() => ''` | Factory for blank items |
| `renderItem` | `(item, index, helpers) => ReactNode` | — | Render each item; helpers: `update`, `remove` |
| `addText` | `ReactNode` | `'Add item'` | Add button label |
| `max` | `number` | — | Hide Add button when reached |
| `min` | `number` | `0` | Hide Remove button when at minimum |
| `disabled` | `boolean` | `false` | Disables all controls |

### ObjectField

Lightweight fieldset with title, description, action slot, collapsible support, and two visual variants.

<ComponentPreview
  name="pro-fields-object-field-demo"
  previewClassName="min-h-[260px] items-start p-6"
  align="start"
/>

| Prop | Type | Default | Description |
|------|------|---------|-------------|
| `title` | `ReactNode` | — | Section heading |
| `description` | `ReactNode` | — | Helper text below title |
| `action` | `ReactNode` | — | Element rendered to the right of the title |
| `variant` | `'separated' \| 'bordered' \| 'none'` | `'separated'` | Visual style |
| `collapsible` | `boolean` | `false` | Whether section can be toggled |
| `defaultOpen` | `boolean` | `true` | Initial open state when collapsible |

c6:T4d9,"use client"

import { createForm } from "@formily/core"
import { Field, FormProvider } from "@formily/react"

import { FormItem } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/form-item"
import { FormilySlider } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/formily-fields"

const form = createForm()

export function ProFieldsSliderDemo() {
  return (
    <FormProvider form={form}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm space-y-6 p-4">
        <Field
          name="volume"
          title="Volume"
          initialValue={40}
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilySlider,
            { min: 0, max: 100, step: 1, showValue: true },
          ]}
        />
        <Field
          name="opacity"
          title="Opacity"
          initialValue={70}
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilySlider,
            { min: 0, max: 100, step: 10, showValue: true },
          ]}
        />
        <Field
          name="disabled"
          title="Disabled"
          initialValue={30}
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilySlider,
            { min: 0, max: 100, disabled: true, showValue: true },
          ]}
        />
      </div>
    </FormProvider>
  )
}

dc:T6d2,"use client"

import { createForm } from "@formily/core"
import { Field, FormProvider } from "@formily/react"

import { FormItem } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/form-item"
import { FormilyCascader } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/formily-fields"

const regionOptions = [
  {
    label: "North America",
    value: "na",
    children: [
      {
        label: "United States",
        value: "us",
        children: [
          { label: "California", value: "ca" },
          { label: "New York", value: "ny" },
          { label: "Texas", value: "tx" },
        ],
      },
      {
        label: "Canada",
        value: "ca-country",
        children: [
          { label: "Ontario", value: "on" },
          { label: "British Columbia", value: "bc" },
        ],
      },
    ],
  },
  {
    label: "Asia",
    value: "asia",
    children: [
      {
        label: "China",
        value: "cn",
        children: [
          { label: "Beijing", value: "bj" },
          { label: "Shanghai", value: "sh" },
        ],
      },
      {
        label: "Japan",
        value: "jp",
        children: [
          { label: "Tokyo", value: "tk" },
          { label: "Osaka", value: "os" },
        ],
      },
    ],
  },
]

const form = createForm()

export function ProFieldsCascaderDemo() {
  return (
    <FormProvider form={form}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm space-y-6 p-4">
        <Field
          name="region"
          title="Region"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyCascader,
            {
              options: regionOptions,
              placeholder: "Select region",
              allowClear: true,
            },
          ]}
        />
      </div>
    </FormProvider>
  )
}

      { label: "UI/UX", value: "uiux" },
      { label: "Brand", value: "brand" },
    ],
  },
  {
    label: "Marketing",
    value: "marketing",
  },
]

const form = createForm()

export function ProFieldsTreeSelectDemo() {
  return (
    <FormProvider form={form}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm space-y-6 p-4">
        <Field
          name="department"
          title="Department (single)"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyTreeSelect,
            {
              options: deptOptions,
              placeholder: "Select department",
              allowClear: true,
            },
          ]}
        />
        <Field
          name="teams"
          title="Teams (multi-select)"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyTreeSelect,
            {
              options: deptOptions,
              placeholder: "Select teams",
              multiple: true,
              allowClear: true,
            },
          ]}
        />
      </div>
    </FormProvider>
  )
}

ec:T480,"use client"

import { createForm } from "@formily/core"
import { Field, FormProvider } from "@formily/react"

import { FormItem } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/form-item"
import { FormilyUpload } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/formily-fields"

const form = createForm()

export function ProFieldsUploadDemo() {
  return (
    <FormProvider form={form}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm space-y-6 p-4">
        <Field
          name="avatar"
          title="Avatar"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyUpload,
            {
              accept: "image/*",
              multiple: false,
              maxCount: 1,
              placeholder: "Click to upload image",
            },
          ]}
        />
        <Field
          name="documents"
          title="Documents"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyUpload,
            {
              accept: ".pdf,.doc,.docx",
              multiple: true,
              maxCount: 5,
              placeholder: "Upload up to 5 documents",
            },
          ]}
        />
      </div>
    </FormProvider>
  )
}

106:T494,"use client"

import { createForm } from "@formily/core"
import { Field, FormProvider } from "@formily/react"

import { FormItem } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/form-item"
import { FormilyMoney } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/formily-fields"

const form = createForm()

export function ProFieldsMoneyDemo() {
  return (
    <FormProvider form={form}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm space-y-6 p-4">
        <Field
          name="price"
          title="Price (USD)"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyMoney,
            { currency: "$", precision: 2, placeholder: "0.00" },
          ]}
        />
        <Field
          name="budget"
          title="Budget (EUR)"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyMoney,
            { currency: "€", precision: 2, placeholder: "0.00" },
          ]}
        />
        <Field
          name="amount"
          title="Amount (JPY)"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyMoney,
            { currency: "¥", precision: 0, placeholder: "0" },
          ]}
        />
      </div>
    </FormProvider>
  )
}

import { createForm } from "@formily/core"
import { Field, FormProvider } from "@formily/react"

import { FormItem } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/form-item"
import { FormilyMoney } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/formily-fields"

const form = createForm()

export function ProFieldsMoneyDemo() {
  return (
    <FormProvider form={form}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm space-y-6 p-4">
        <Field
          name="price"
          title="Price (USD)"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyMoney,
            { currency: "$", precision: 2, placeholder: "0.00" },
          ]}
        />
        <Field
          name="budget"
          title="Budget (EUR)"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyMoney,
            { currency: "€", precision: 2, placeholder: "0.00" },
          ]}
        />
        <Field
          name="amount"
          title="Amount (JPY)"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyMoney,
            { currency: "¥", precision: 0, placeholder: "0" },
          ]}
        />
      </div>
    </FormProvider>
  )
}

135:T549,"use client"

import { createForm } from "@formily/core"
import { Field, FormProvider } from "@formily/react"

import { FormItem } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/form-item"
import { FormilySegmented } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/formily-fields"

const form = createForm()

export function ProFieldsSegmentedDemo() {
  return (
    <FormProvider form={form}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm space-y-6 p-4">
        <Field
          name="view"
          title="View"
          initialValue="list"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilySegmented,
            {
              options: [
                { label: "List", value: "list" },
                { label: "Board", value: "board" },
                { label: "Calendar", value: "calendar" },
              ],
            },
          ]}
        />
        <Field
          name="size"
          title="Size"
          initialValue="md"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilySegmented,
            {
              options: [
                { label: "S", value: "sm" },
                { label: "M", value: "md" },
                { label: "L", value: "lg" },
                { label: "XL", value: "xl", disabled: true },
              ],
            },
          ]}
        />
      </div>
    </FormProvider>
  )
}

13b:T4d9,"use client"

import { createForm } from "@formily/core"
import { Field, FormProvider } from "@formily/react"

import { FormItem } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/form-item"
import { FormilySlider } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/formily-fields"

const form = createForm()

export function ProFieldsSliderDemo() {
  return (
    <FormProvider form={form}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm space-y-6 p-4">
        <Field
          name="volume"
          title="Volume"
          initialValue={40}
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilySlider,
            { min: 0, max: 100, step: 1, showValue: true },
          ]}
        />
        <Field
          name="opacity"
          title="Opacity"
          initialValue={70}
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilySlider,
            { min: 0, max: 100, step: 10, showValue: true },
          ]}
        />
        <Field
          name="disabled"
          title="Disabled"
          initialValue={30}
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilySlider,
            { min: 0, max: 100, disabled: true, showValue: true },
          ]}
        />
      </div>
    </FormProvider>
  )
}

13e:T407,"use client"

import { createForm } from "@formily/core"
import { Field, FormProvider } from "@formily/react"

import { FormItem } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/form-item"
import { FormilyRate } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/formily-fields"

const form = createForm()

export function ProFieldsRateDemo() {
  return (
    <FormProvider form={form}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm space-y-6 p-4">
        <Field
          name="rating"
          title="Rating"
          initialValue={3}
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[FormilyRate, { count: 5 }]}
        />
        <Field
          name="difficulty"
          title="Difficulty (10-star)"
          initialValue={7}
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[FormilyRate, { count: 10 }]}
        />
        <Field
          name="readonly"
          title="Read-only"
          initialValue={4}
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[FormilyRate, { disabled: true }]}
        />
      </div>
    </FormProvider>
  )
}

14d:T6d2,"use client"

import { createForm } from "@formily/core"
import { Field, FormProvider } from "@formily/react"

import { FormItem } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/form-item"
import { FormilyCascader } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/formily-fields"

const regionOptions = [
  {
    label: "North America",
    value: "na",
    children: [
      {
        label: "United States",
        value: "us",
        children: [
          { label: "California", value: "ca" },
          { label: "New York", value: "ny" },
          { label: "Texas", value: "tx" },
        ],
      },
      {
        label: "Canada",
        value: "ca-country",
        children: [
          { label: "Ontario", value: "on" },
          { label: "British Columbia", value: "bc" },
        ],
      },
    ],
  },
  {
    label: "Asia",
    value: "asia",
    children: [
      {
        label: "China",
        value: "cn",
        children: [
          { label: "Beijing", value: "bj" },
          { label: "Shanghai", value: "sh" },
        ],
      },
      {
        label: "Japan",
        value: "jp",
        children: [
          { label: "Tokyo", value: "tk" },
          { label: "Osaka", value: "os" },
        ],
      },
    ],
  },
]

const form = createForm()

export function ProFieldsCascaderDemo() {
  return (
    <FormProvider form={form}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm space-y-6 p-4">
        <Field
          name="region"
          title="Region"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyCascader,
            {
              options: regionOptions,
              placeholder: "Select region",
              allowClear: true,
            },
          ]}
        />
      </div>
    </FormProvider>
  )
}

156:T646,"use client"

import { createForm } from "@formily/core"
import { Field, FormProvider } from "@formily/react"

import { FormItem } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/form-item"
import { FormilyTreeSelect } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/formily-fields"

const deptOptions = [
  {
    label: "Engineering",
    value: "eng",
    children: [
      { label: "Frontend", value: "frontend" },
      { label: "Backend", value: "backend" },
      { label: "DevOps", value: "devops" },
    ],
  },
  {
    label: "Design",
    value: "design",
    children: [
      { label: "UI/UX", value: "uiux" },
      { label: "Brand", value: "brand" },
    ],
  },
  {
    label: "Marketing",
    value: "marketing",
  },
]

const form = createForm()

export function ProFieldsTreeSelectDemo() {
  return (
    <FormProvider form={form}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm space-y-6 p-4">
        <Field
          name="department"
          title="Department (single)"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyTreeSelect,
            {
              options: deptOptions,
              placeholder: "Select department",
              allowClear: true,
            },
          ]}
        />
        <Field
          name="teams"
          title="Teams (multi-select)"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyTreeSelect,
            {
              options: deptOptions,
              placeholder: "Select teams",
              multiple: true,
              allowClear: true,
            },
          ]}
        />
      </div>
    </FormProvider>
  )
}

160:T480,"use client"

import { createForm } from "@formily/core"
import { Field, FormProvider } from "@formily/react"

import { FormItem } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/form-item"
import { FormilyUpload } from "@/components/pro/pro-form/formily-fields"

const form = createForm()

export function ProFieldsUploadDemo() {
  return (
    <FormProvider form={form}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm space-y-6 p-4">
        <Field
          name="avatar"
          title="Avatar"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyUpload,
            {
              accept: "image/*",
              multiple: false,
              maxCount: 1,
              placeholder: "Click to upload image",
            },
          ]}
        />
        <Field
          name="documents"
          title="Documents"
          decorator={[FormItem]}
          component={[
            FormilyUpload,
            {
              accept: ".pdf,.doc,.docx",
              multiple: true,
              maxCount: 5,
              placeholder: "Upload up to 5 documents",
            },
          ]}
        />
      </div>
    </FormProvider>
  )
}

166:T473,"use client"

import { useState } from "react"

import { ArrayField } from "@/components/pro/pro-fields/array-field"
import { Input } from "@/components/pro/pro-fields/input"

interface Contact {
  name: string
  email: string
}

export function ProFieldsArrayFieldDemo() {
  const [value, setValue] = useState<Contact[]>([
    { name: "Alice Wang", email: "alice@example.com" },
    { name: "Bob Chen", email: "bob@example.com" },
  ])

  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-md p-4">
      <ArrayField<Contact>
        value={value}
        onChange={setValue}
        newItem={() => ({ name: "", email: "" })}
        addText="Add contact"
        min={1}
        renderItem={(item, _index, { update }) => (
          <div className="space-y-2">
            <Input
              placeholder="Name"
              value={item.name}
              onChange={(e) => update({ name: e.target.value })}
            />
            <Input
              placeholder="Email"
              value={item.email}
              onChange={(e) => update({ email: e.target.value })}
            />
          </div>
        )}
      />
    </div>
  )
}

import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button"
import { Input } from "@/components/pro/pro-fields/input"
import { ObjectField } from "@/components/pro/pro-fields/object-field"
import { Select } from "@/components/pro/pro-fields/select"

export function ProFieldsObjectFieldDemo() {
  return (
    <div className="w-full max-w-md space-y-6 p-4">
      {/* Default: separated variant */}
      <ObjectField
        title="Profile"
        description="Your public display information."
        action={<Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="h-6 text-xs">Edit</Button>}
      >
        <Input placeholder="Display name" />
        <Select
          placeholder="Department"
          options={[
            { label: "Product", value: "product" },
            { label: "Engineering", value: "engineering" },
          ]}
        />
      </ObjectField>

      {/* Bordered + collapsible */}
      <ObjectField
        title="Advanced settings"
        description="Only change if you know what you're doing."
        variant="bordered"
        collapsible
        defaultOpen={false}
      >
        <Input placeholder="Custom domain" />
        <Input placeholder="Webhook URL" />
      </ObjectField>
    </div>
  )
}
